Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Colossus 249 (Apollo 9) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 055 OF AGC PROGRAM COMANCHE BY NASA 2021113-051
	10:28 APR.  1,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

001627,000002:                                                                                                  #  Copyright:    Public domain.
001628,000003:                                                                                                  #  Filename:     ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001629,000004:                                                                                                  #  Purpose:      Part of the source code for Colossus 2A, AKA Comanche 055.
001630,000005:                                                                                                  #                It is part of the source code for the Command Module's (CM)
001631,000006:                                                                                                  #                Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), for Apollo 11.
001632,000007:                                                                                                  #  Assembler:    yaYUL
001633,000008:                                                                                                  #  Contact:      Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001634,000009:                                                                                                  #  Website:      www.ibiblio.org/apollo.
001635,000010:                                                                                                  #  Mod history:  2009-05-06 RSB  Started adapting from the Colossus249/ file 
001636,000011:                                                                                                  #                                of the same name, using Comanche055 page 
001637,000012:                                                                                                  #                                images. Only through page 51 so far.
001638,000013:                                                                                                  #                2009-05-07 RSB  Through page 92 so far.
001639,000014:                                                                                                  #                2009-05-07 RSB  (Again!) First draft completed.
001640,000015:                                                                                                  #                2009-05-20 RSB  Fixed some bugs uncovered in trial assemblies:
001641,000016:                                                                                                  #                                EMDOT, STATEXIT, VGDISP, DVPREV, POSTCDH,
001642,000017:                                                                                                  #                                RETROFLG not defined correctly, changed the
001643,000018:                                                                                                  #                                typing of labels 9X9LOC1 and 9X9LOC2, 
001644,000019:                                                                                                  #                                R32FLBIT -> R31FLBIT.
001645,000020:                                                                                                  #                2009-05-21 RSB  Corrected definition of DELBRTMP, which 
001646,000021:                                                                                                  #                                chained to quite a lot of off-by-one errors.
001647,000022:                                                                                                  #                                Changed a +8 to a +8D.
001648,000023:                                                                                                  #                2010-08-24 JL   Fixed page numbers. Added missing comment character. Fixed page number comment.
001649,000024:                                                                                                  #                2011-05-08 JL   Removed workarounds.
001650,000025: 
001651,000026:                                                                                                  #  This source code has been transcribed or otherwise adapted from digitized
001652,000027:                                                                                                  #  images of a hardcopy from the MIT Museum.  The digitization was performed
001653,000028:                                                                                                  #  by Paul Fjeld, and arranged for by Deborah Douglas of the Museum.  Many
001654,000029:                                                                                                  #  thanks to both.  The images (with suitable reduction in storage size and
001655,000030:                                                                                                  #  consequent reduction in image quality as well) are available online at
001656,000031:                                                                                                  #  www.ibiblio.org/apollo.  If for some reason you find that the images are
001657,000032:                                                                                                  #  illegible, contact me at info@sandroid.org about getting access to the 
001658,000033:                                                                                                  #  (much) higher-quality images which Paul actually created.
001659,000034: 
001660,000035:                                                                                                  #  Notations on the hardcopy document read, in part:
001661,000036: 
001662,000037:                                                                                                  #        Assemble revision 055 of AGC program Comanche by NASA
001663,000038:                                                                                                  #        2021113-051.  10:28 APR. 1, 1969  
001664,000039: 
001665,000040:                                                                                                  #        This AGC program shall also be referred to as
001666,000041:                                                                                                  #                        Colossus 2A
001667,000042: 
001668,000043: 
001669,000044:                                                                                                  #  Page 37
001670,000045:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001671,000046: 
001672,000047:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001673,000048:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001674,000049:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE:
001675,000050: 
001676,000051:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001677,000052:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001678,000053:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001679,000054: 
001680,000055:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.
001681,000056:                                                                                                  #                SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y.
001682,000057:                                                                                                  #                USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D, ETC.)
001683,000058: 
001684,000059:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001685,000060:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE:
001686,000061: 
001687,000062:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001688,000063: 
001689,000064:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001690,000065:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING.)  EXAMPLE:
001691,000066: 
001692,000067:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001693,000068: 
001694,000069:                                                                                                  #        THE SIE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001695,000070:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM:  M(SIZE)N.
001696,000071: 
001697,000072:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001698,000073:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001699,000074:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001700,000075:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001701,000076:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001702,000077:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001703,000078: 
001704,000079:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001705,000080: 
001706,000081:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OF PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001707,000082:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001708,000083:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001709,000084:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT.  IE., IT
001710,000085:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001711,000086:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001712,000087:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001713,000088:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001714,000089:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001715,000090:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001716,000091:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS
001717,000092:                                                                                                  #  Page 38
001718,000093:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITHANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001719,000094:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL
001720,000095:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001721,000096:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001722,000097:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001723,000098:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001724,000099: 
001725,000100:                                                                                                  #  Page 39
001726,000101: 
001727,000102:                                                                                                  #  SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001728,000103: 
001729,000104: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001730,000105: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS
001731,000106: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001732,000107: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001733,000108: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001734,000109: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001735,000110: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001736,000111:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001737,000112: 
001738,000113: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE
001739,000114: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001740,000115: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001741,000116: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001742,000117: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001743,000118: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001744,000119: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001745,000120: 
001746,000121: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20                                    
001747,000122: 37,2001                        SR                 EQUALS   21                                    
001748,000123: 37,2001                        CYL                EQUALS   22                                    
001749,000124: 37,2001                        EDOP               EQUALS   23                                    #  EDITS INTERPRETIVE OPERATION CODE PAIRS.
001750,000125: 
001751,000126: 37,2001                        TIME2              EQUALS   24                                    
001752,000127: 37,2001                        TIME1              EQUALS   25                                    
001753,000128: 37,2001                        TIME3              EQUALS   26                                    
001754,000129: 37,2001                        TIME4              EQUALS   27                                    
001755,000130: 37,2001                        TIME5              EQUALS   30                                    
001756,000131: 37,2001                        TIME6              EQUALS   31                                    
001757,000132: 37,2001                        CDUX               EQUALS   32                                    
001758,000133: 37,2001                        CDUY               EQUALS   33                                    
001759,000134: 37,2001                        CDUZ               EQUALS   34                                    
001760,000135: 37,2001                        CDUT               EQUALS   35                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION CDU (WAS OPTY).
001761,000136: 37,2001  0000035               OPTY               =        CDUT                                  
001762,000137: 37,2001                        CDUS               EQUALS   36                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT CDU (WAS OPTX).
001763,000138: 37,2001  0000036               OPTX               =        CDUS                                  
001764,000139: 37,2001                        PIPAX              EQUALS   37                                    
001765,000140: 37,2001                        PIPAY              EQUALS   40                                    
001766,000141: 37,2001                        PIPAZ              EQUALS   41                                    
001767,000142: 37,2001                        BMAGX              EQUALS   42                                    
001768,000143: 37,2001                        BMAGY              EQUALS   43                                    
001769,000144: 37,2001                        BMAGZ              EQUALS   44                                    
001770,000145: 37,2001                        INLINK             EQUALS   45                                    
001771,000146: 37,2001                        RNRAD              EQUALS   46                                    
001772,000147: 37,2001                        GYROCTR            EQUALS   47                                    
001773,000148: 37,2001                        GYROCMD            EQUALS   47                                    
001774,000149: 37,2001                        CDUXCMD            EQUALS   50                                    
001775,000150: 37,2001                        CDUYCMD            EQUALS   51                                    
001776,000151: 
001777,000152:                                                                                                  #  Page 40
001778,000153: 
001779,000154: 37,2001                        CDUZCMD            EQUALS   52                                    
001780,000155: 37,2001                        CDUTCMD            EQUALS   53                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION COMMAND (WAS OPTYCMD)
001781,000156: 37,2001  0000053               OPTYCMD            =        CDUTCMD                               
001782,000157: 37,2001  0000053               TVCYAW             EQUALS   CDUTCMD                               #  SPS YAW COMMAND IN TVC MODE
001783,000158: 37,2001                        CDUSCMD            EQUALS   54                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT COMMAND (WAS OPTXCMD).
001784,000159: 37,2001  0000054               TVCPITCH           EQUALS   CDUSCMD                               #  SPS PITCH COMMAND IN TVC MODE
001785,000160: 37,2001  0000054               OPTXCMD            =        CDUSCMD                               
001786,000161: 37,2001                        EMSD               EQUALS   55                                    
001787,000162: 37,2001                        THRUST             EQUALS   55                                    
001788,000163: 37,2001                        LEMONM             EQUALS   56                                    
001789,000164: 37,2001                        LOCALARM           EQUALS   57                                    
001790,000165: 37,2001                        BANKALRM           EQUALS   60                                    
001791,000166: 
001792,000167:                                                                                                  #  INTERPRETIVE REGISTERS ADDRESSED RELATIVE TO VAC AREA.
001793,000168: 
001794,000169: 37,2001                        LVSQUARE           EQUALS   34D                                   #  SQUARE OF VECTOR INPUT TO ABVAL AND UNIT
001795,000170: 37,2001                        LV                 EQUALS   36D                                   #  LENGTH OF VECTOR INPUT TO UNIT.
001796,000171: 37,2001                        X1                 EQUALS   38D                                   #  INTERPRETIVE SPECIAL REGISTER RELATIVE
001797,000172: 37,2001                        X2                 EQUALS   39D                                   #  TO THE WORK AREA.
001798,000173: 37,2001                        S1                 EQUALS   40D                                   
001799,000174: 37,2001                        S2                 EQUALS   41D                                   
001800,000175: 37,2001                        QPRET              EQUALS   42D
